     C           YBRDC     ANDNE'N'
     C                     MOVE 'Y'       YBRDC
     C                     ENDIF
      * If changed update record otherwise release record
     C           YBRDC     IFEQ 'Y'
     C                     UPDAT@MOCPWJ                91  *
     C                     ELSE
      * Release record lock

     C                     ENDIF

      * Change error detected

     C                     ELSE

      * DBF change successful
     C                     ENDIF
